<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Display hierarchical data in a tree structure</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Expand or collapse nodes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports keyboard navigation</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Select single or multiple nodes (depending on the selection mode)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Perform actions on the nodes, such as deleting them or performing some other
operation</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the tree view package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> tree</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tree-view&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>The tree view package exports two key functions:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>
<h3 id="create-the-tree-collection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Create the tree collection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#create-the-tree-collection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code> function to create a tree collection. This creates a tree
factory that the component uses for traversal.</p>
<pre class="prose language-ts"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">import</span> <span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword">as</span> tree <span class="token keyword">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/tree-view&quot;</span>

<h3 id="create-the-tree-view" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Create the tree view<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#create-the-tree-view"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Pass the tree collection to the machine to create the tree view.</p>

<h3 id="expanding-and-collapsing-nodes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Expanding and Collapsing Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#expanding-and-collapsing-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the tree view will expand or collapse when clicking the branch
control. To control the expanded state of the tree view, use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.expand</code>
and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.collapse</code> methods.</p>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Note:</strong> The array parameter contains individual node values/IDs, not paths.
All nodes specified in the array will be collapsed or expanded.</p>
</blockquote>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">expand</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/zag-js&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// expand a single node by its value/ID</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">expand</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/zag-js&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/pandacss&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// expand multiple nodes by their values/IDs</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">expand</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// expand all nodes</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collapse</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/@types&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// collapse a single node by its value/ID</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collapse</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/@types&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/pandacss&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// collapse multiple nodes by their values/IDs</span>
</span><span class="code-line">api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collapse</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token comment">// collapse all nodes</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="multiple-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Multiple selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#multiple-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tree view supports multiple selection. To enable this, set the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionMode</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">multiple</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  selectionMode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;multiple&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-default-expanded-nodes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the default expanded nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-default-expanded-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the default expanded nodes, use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultExpandedValue</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  defaultExpandedValue<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;node_modules/pandacss&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="setting-the-default-selected-nodes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting the default selected nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-the-default-selected-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To set the default selected nodes, use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSelectedValue</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-expanded-and-selected-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled expanded and selected values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-expanded-and-selected-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use controlled props when expansion or selection is managed externally.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="indentation-guide" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Indentation Guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#indentation-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When rendering a branch node in the tree view, you can render the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">indentGuide</code>
element by using the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api.getBranchIndentGuideProps()</code> function.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getBranchProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nodeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">  </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span>div</span> <span class="token spread"><span class="token punctuation">{</span><span class="token spread operator">...</span>api<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">getBranchControlProps</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>nodeProps<span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token punctuation">&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token tag"><span class="token tag"><span class="token punctuation">&lt;</span><span class="token class-name">FolderIcon</span></span> <span class="token punctuation">/&gt;</span></span><span class="token plain-text">
</span></span><span class="code-line"><span class="token plain-text">    </span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>node<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token plain-text">

<h3 id="listening-for-selection" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for selection<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-selection"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a node is selected, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onSelectionChange</code> callback is invoked with the
selected nodes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;selected nodes:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">selectedNodes</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-expanding-and-collapsing" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for expanding and collapsing<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-expanding-and-collapsing"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When a node is expanded or collapsed, the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onExpandedChange</code> callback is invoked
with the expanded nodes.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-focus-and-checked-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for focus and checked changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-focus-and-checked-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onFocusChange</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onCheckedChange</code> when you need focus/checkbox state.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { checkedValue: string[] }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">checkedValue</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>

<h3 id="programmatic-tree-control" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Programmatic tree control<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#programmatic-tree-control"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<h3 id="controlling-branch-click-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling branch click behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-branch-click-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">expandOnClick</code> to control whether clicking a branch toggles expansion.</p>

<h3 id="controlling-typeahead" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling typeahead<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-typeahead"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>

<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>

<h3 id="lazy-loading" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Lazy Loading<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#lazy-loading"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p><strong>Added in v1.15.0</strong></p>
</blockquote>
<p>Lazy loading is a feature that allows the tree view to load children of a node
on demand. This helps to improve the initial load time and memory usage.</p>
<p>To use this, you need to provide the following:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">loadChildren</code> — A function that is used to load the children of a node.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onLoadChildrenComplete</code> — A callback that is called when the children of a
node are loaded. Used to update the tree collection.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onLoadChildrenError</code> — A callback that is called when loading fails.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">childrenCount</code> — A number that indicates the number of children of a branch
node.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">function</span> <span class="token function">TreeAsync</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span> setCollection<span class="token punctuation">]</span> <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useState</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">collection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">id</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function-variable function">nodeToString</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> node<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      rootNode<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;ROOT&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        children<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;node_modules&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;node_modules&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> childrenCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">3</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">          <span class="token punctuation">{</span> id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;src&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> name<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;src&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> childrenCount<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">2</span> <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">        <span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    id<span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token function">useId</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token keyword">async</span> <span class="token function">loadChildren</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> valuePath<span class="token punctuation">,</span> signal <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">const</span> url <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">/api/file-system/</span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>valuePath<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token function">join</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;/&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">const</span> response <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> <span class="token function">fetch</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>url<span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span> signal <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">const</span> data <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token keyword">await</span> response<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">json</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token keyword">return</span> data<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">children</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">onLoadChildrenComplete</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> collection <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token function">setCollection</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>collection<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function">onLoadChildrenError</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token punctuation">{</span> nodes <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">      <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">error</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Failed to load:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> nodes<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">// ...</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="renaming-nodes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Renaming Nodes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#renaming-nodes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tree view supports renaming node labels inline, perfect for file explorers,
content management systems, and other applications where users need to edit item
names.</p>
<p>To enable renaming:</p>
<ol>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Add the rename input to your tree node component</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Handle the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRenameComplete</code> callback to update your collection</li>
</ol>

<h3 id="controlling-which-nodes-can-be-renamed" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlling which nodes can be renamed<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlling-which-nodes-can-be-renamed"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">canRename</code> callback to control which nodes are renameable based on node
type or custom logic.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">canRename</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>node<span class="token punctuation">,</span> indexPath<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// Only allow renaming leaf nodes (files), not branches (folders)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>node<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">children</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="validating-rename-input" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Validating rename input<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#validating-rename-input"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onBeforeRename</code> callback to validate the new name before accepting the
change. Return <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">false</code> to reject the rename.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onBeforeRename</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// Prevent empty names (label is already trimmed)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">if</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token operator">!</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">label</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token boolean">false</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token comment">// Prevent duplicate names</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> parent <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">getParentNode</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">indexPath</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">const</span> hasDuplicate <span class="token operator">=</span> parent<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">children</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">some</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">      <span class="token punctuation">(</span>child<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> child<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span> <span class="token operator">===</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">label</span> <span class="token operator">&amp;&amp;</span> child<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">id</span> <span class="token operator">!==</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token keyword">return</span> <span class="token operator">!</span>hasDuplicate
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="tracking-rename-events" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Tracking rename events<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#tracking-rename-events"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onRenameStart</code> callback to track when users start renaming, useful for
analytics or showing contextual hints.</p>
<pre class="prose language-tsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>tree<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  collection<span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token function">onRenameStart</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>details<span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;Started renaming:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">node</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">name</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">    <span class="token function">trackEvent</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;tree_rename_started&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p><strong>Features:</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Press <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">F2</code> to enter rename mode</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Press <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Enter</code> to submit or <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">Escape</code> to cancel</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Blur automatically submits changes</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Empty or whitespace-only names are automatically rejected</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Labels are automatically trimmed before callbacks</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">IME composition events are properly handled</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-renaming</code> attribute added for styling</li>
</ul>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tree view machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">TreeCollection&lt;T&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The tree collection data</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; tree: string; label: string; node: (value: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the tree elements. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">expandedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled expanded node ids</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultExpandedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial expanded node ids when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the expanded node value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled selected node value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultSelectedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial selected node value when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the selected node value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultCheckedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The initial checked node value when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the checked node value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">checkedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The controlled checked node value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultFocusedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The initial focused node value when rendered.
Use when you don&#x27;t need to control the focused node value.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">focusedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The value of the focused node</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectionMode</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">&quot;single&quot; | &quot;multiple&quot;</code><span class="d_block">Whether the tree supports multiple selection
- &quot;single&quot;: only one node can be selected
- &quot;multiple&quot;: multiple nodes can be selected</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onExpandedChange</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(details: ExpandedChangeDetails&lt;T&gt;) =&gt; boolean</code><span class="d_block">Called before a rename is completed. E.x.: Iframes, Electron.</span></li></ul>
<h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The tree view <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collection</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">TreeCollection&lt;V&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The tree collection data</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">expandedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The value of the expanded nodes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setExpandedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the expanded value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The value of the selected nodes.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setSelectedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the selected value</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">checkedValue</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string[]</code><span class="d_block">The value of the checked nodes</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">toggleChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string, isBranch: boolean) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Toggles the checked value of a node</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">setChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Sets the checked value of a node</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">clearChecked</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">VoidFunction</code><span class="d_block">Clears the checked value of a node</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">getCheckedMap</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">() =&gt; VisibleNode&lt;V&gt;[]</code><span class="d_block">Returns the visible nodes as a flat array of nodes and their index path.
Useful for rendering virtualized tree views.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">expand</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value?: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to expand nodes.
If no value is provided, all nodes will be expanded</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">collapse</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value?: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to collapse nodes
If no value is provided, all nodes will be collapsed</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">select</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">(value?: string[]) =&gt; void</code><span class="d_block">Function to select nodes

<h3 id="css-variables" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">CSS Variables<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#css-variables"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Item</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--depth</kbd></div><span>The depth value for the Item</span></div></div></div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_4 py_4"><div class="fw_semibold">Branch</div><div class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_4 max-w_lg"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8 flex-d_row w_full"><div class="min-w_160px"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">--depth</kbd></div><span>The depth value for the Branch</span></div></div></div></div>
<h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Adheres to the
<a target="_blank" rel="noopener" href="https://www.w3.org/WAI/ARIA/apg/patterns/treeview" class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px">Tree View WAI-ARIA design pattern</a>.</p>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Tab</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the tree view, placing the first tree view item in focus.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Enter</kbd><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Space</kbd></div><div>Selects the item or branch node</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the next node</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the previous node</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowRight</kbd></div><div>When focus is on a closed branch node, opens the branch.<br> When focus is on an open branch node, moves focus to the first item node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">ArrowLeft</kbd></div><div>When focus is on an open branch node, closes the node.<br> When focus is on an item or branch node, moves focus to its parent branch node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Home</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to first node without opening or closing a node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">End</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to the last node that can be focused without expanding any nodes that are closed.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">a-z</kbd><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">A-Z</kbd></div><div>Focus moves to the next node with a name that starts with the typed character. The search logic ignores nodes that are descendants of closed branch.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">*</kbd></div><div>Expands all sibling nodes that are at the same depth as the focused node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Shift + ArrowDown</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to and toggles the selection state of the next node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Shift + ArrowUp</kbd></div><div>Moves focus to and toggles the selection state of the previous node.</div></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd class="ff_mono d_inline-block px_0.4em py_0.1em fs_0.8em fw_bold bg_bg.code.inline/50 c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 bd-w_1px bd-b-w_2px bd-c_border.bold bdr_3px">Ctrl + A</kbd></div><div>Selects all nodes in the tree. If all nodes are selected, unselects all nodes.</div></li></ul><a href="https://github.com/chakra-ui/zag/edit/main/website/data/components/tree-view.mdx" class="d_inline-flex ai_center gap_1 TreeView component provides a hierarchical view of data, similar to a file\nsystem explorer. It allows users to expand and collapse branches, select\nindividual or multiple nodes, and traverse the hierarchy using keyboard\nnavigation.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/tree-view\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"TreeView\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eDisplay hierarchical data in a tree structure\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eExpand or collapse nodes\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports keyboard navigation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSelect single or multiple nodes (depending on the selection mode)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePerform actions on the nodes, such as deleting them or performing some other\noperation\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the tree view package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tree-view/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the tree view anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"tree-view\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the tree view package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as tree from \"@zag-js/tree-view\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tree view package exports two key functions:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCreate the tree collection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003ecollection\u003c/code\u003e function to create a tree collection. This creates a tree\nfactory that the component uses for traversal.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-ts\"\u003eimport * as tree from \"@zag-js/tree-view\"\n\ninterface Node {\n  id: string\n  name: string\n  children?: Node[]\n}\n\nconst collection = tree.collection\u0026#x3C;Node\u003e({\n  nodeToValue: (node) =\u003e node.id,\n  nodeToString: (node) =\u003e node.name,\n  rootNode: {\n    id: \"ROOT\",\n    name: \"\",\n    children: [\n      {\n        id: \"node_modules\",\n        name: \"node_modules\",\n        children: [\n          { id: \"node_modules/zag-js\", name: \"zag-js\" },\n          { id: \"node_modules/pandacss\", name: \"panda\" },\n          {\n            id: \"node_modules/@types\",\n            name: \"@types\",\n            children: [\n              { id: \"node_modules/@types/react\", name: \"react\" },\n              { id: \"node_modules/@types/react-dom\", name: \"react-dom\" },\n            ],\n          },\n        ],\n      },\n    ],\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCreate the tree view\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003ePass the tree collection to the machine to create the tree view.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"tree-view/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eExpanding and Collapsing Nodes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the tree view will expand or collapse when clicking the branch\ncontrol. To control the expanded state of the tree view, use the \u003ccode\u003eapi.expand\u003c/code\u003e\nand \u003ccode\u003eapi.collapse\u003c/code\u003e methods.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eNote:\u003c/strong\u003e The array parameter contains individual node values/IDs, not paths.\nAll nodes specified in the array will be collapsed or expanded.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003eapi.expand([\"node_modules/zag-js\"]) // expand a single node by its value/ID\napi.expand([\"node_modules/zag-js\", \"node_modules/pandacss\"]) // expand multiple nodes by their values/IDs\napi.expand() // expand all nodes\n\napi.collapse([\"node_modules/@types\"]) // collapse a single node by its value/ID\napi.collapse([\"node_modules/@types\", \"node_modules/pandacss\"]) // collapse multiple nodes by their values/IDs\napi.collapse() // collapse all nodes\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eMultiple selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tree view supports multiple selection. [\"node_modules/pandacss\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled expanded and selected values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse controlled props when expansion or selection onExpandedChange(details) {\n    setExpandedValue(details.expandedValue)\n  },\n  onSelectionChange(details) {\n    setSelectedValue(details.selectedValue)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eIndentation Guide\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen rendering a branch node in the tree view, you can render the class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{9}\"\u003e\u0026#x3C;div {...api.getBranchProps(nodeProps)}\u003e\n  \u0026#x3C;div {...api.getBranchControlProps(nodeProps)}\u003e\n    \u0026#x3C;FolderIcon \u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n\u0026#x3C;/div\u003e\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for selection\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen a node is selected, the \u003ccode\u003eonSelectionChange\u003c/code\u003e callback is invoked with the\nselected nodes.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2-5}\"\u003econst service onFocusChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { focusedValue, focusedNode }\n    console.log(details.focusedValue)\n  },\n  onCheckedChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { checkedValue: false,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eLazy Loading\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eAdded in v1.15.0\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eLazy loading is a feature that allows the tree view to load children of a node\non demand. This helps to improve the initial load time and memory usage.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo use this, you need to provide the following:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eloadChildren\u003c/code\u003e — A function that is used to load the children of a node.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonLoadChildrenComplete\u003c/code\u003e — A callback that is called when the children of a\nnode are loaded. Used to update the tree collection.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonLoadChildrenError\u003c/code\u003e — A callback that is called when loading fails.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003echildrenCount\u003c/code\u003e — A number that indicates the number of children of a branch\nnode.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\"\u003efunction TreeAsync() {\n  const [collection, setCollection] = useState(\n    tree.collection({\n      nodeToValue: (node) =\u003e node.id,\n      nodeToString: (node) =\u003e node.name,\n      rootNode: {\n        id: \"ROOT\",\n        name: \"\",\n        children: [\n          { id: \"node_modules\", name: \"node_modules\", childrenCount: 3 },\n          { id: \"src\", name: \"src\", childrenCount: 2 },\n        ],\n      },\n    }),\n  )\n\n  const service = useMachine(tree.machine, {\n    id: useId(),\n    collection,\n    async loadChildren({ valuePath, signal }) {\n      const url = `/api/file-system/${valuePath.join(\"/\")}`\n      const response = await fetch(url, { signal })\n      const data = await response.json()\n      return data.children\n    },\n    onLoadChildrenComplete({ collection }) {\n      setCollection(collection)\n    },\n    onLoadChildrenError({ nodes }) {\n      console.error(\"Failed to load:\", nodes)\n    },\n  })\n\n  // ...\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRenaming Nodes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe tree view supports renaming node labels inline, perfect for file explorers,\ncontent management systems, and other applications where users need to edit item\nnames.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo enable renaming:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003col\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAdd the rename input to your tree node component\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eHandle the which nodes can be renamed\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003ecanRename\u003c/code\u003e callback to control which nodes are renameable based on node\ntype or custom logic.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{3-6}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tree.machine, {\n  collection,\n  canRename(node, indexPath) {\n    // Only allow renaming leaf nodes (files), not branches (folders)\n    return !node.children\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eValidating rename input\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003eonBeforeRename\u003c/code\u003e callback to validate the new name before accepting the\nchange. Return \u003ccode\u003efalse\u003c/code\u003e to reject the rename.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{3-14}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(tree.machine, {\n  collection,\n  onBeforeRename(details) {\n    // Prevent empty names (label is already trimmed)\n    if (!details.label) return false\n\n    // Prevent duplicate names\n    const parent = getParentNode(details.indexPath)\n    const hasDuplicate = parent.children.some(\n      (child) =\u003e child.name === details.label \u0026#x26;\u0026#x26; child.id !== details.value,\n    )\n    return !hasDuplicate\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eTracking rename events\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003eonRenameStart\u003c/code\u003e callback to track when users start renaming, useful for\nanalytics or showing contextual hints.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-tsx\" metastring=\"{3-6}\"\u003econst service = },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures:\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003ePress \u003ccode\u003eF2\u003c/code\u003e to enter
